10315,"""""""

def get_condition(question):
    """"""
    This function extracts the condition value of a given question.

    Parameters
    ----------
    question : str
        The question to be parsed.

    Returns
    -------
    condition : str
        The extracted condition value.
    """"""
    
    # Split the question into words
    words = question.split()
    
    # Find the index of the word 'is' in the list of words
    idx = words.index('is')
    
    # Get the condition value by slicing the list of words after the index of 'is'
    condition = "" "".join(words[idx+1:])
    
    return condition


def generate_query(field_name, condition):
    """"""
    This function generates an Elasticsearch query string based on the 
    provided field name and condition value.

    Parameters
    ----------
    field_name : str
        The name of the field to search.
    condition : str
        The condition value to filter results by.

    Returns"

10362,"""""""

def get_es_client():
    es = None
    try:
        es = Elasticsearch([{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}])
        if not es.ping():
            raise ConnectionError(""Elasticsearch service unavailable"")
    except Exception as e:
        print(e)

    return es


def search_by_field_value(es, index, field_name, field_value):
    """"""
    Search by field name and field value
    :param es: elasticsearch client instance
    :param index: index to be searched in
    :param field_name: field name of the document
    :param field_value: field value of the document
    :return: list of documents matching the criteria
    """"""
    body = {
        ""query"": {
            ""match"": {
                field_name: field_value
            }
        },
        ""_source"": [""*""]
    }
    res = es.search(index=index"

def get_es_client():
    es = None
    try:
        # Connect to local elasticsearch instance
        es = Elasticsearch()
    except Exception as e:
        print(""Connection failed"",e)

    return es


def search(es):
    res = es.search(index=""vaersdata"", body={
        ""query"": {
            ""match"": {""STATE"":""MO""}
        }
    })
    print('Got %d Hits:' % len(res['hits']['hits']))
    for hit in res['hits']['hits']:
        print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text)s"" % hit[""_source""])

if __name__ == ""__main__"":
    es = get_es_client()
    if not es:
        exit(-1)
    search(es)"

    })

11214,"""""""

def get_es_client():
    es = None
    try:
        # Connect to local elasticsearch instance
        es = Elasticsearch([{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}])

        if not es.ping():
            raise ConnectionError(""Elasticsearch service unavailable"")

    except Exception as e:
        print(e)
        sys.exit()

    return es


def search_by_field_value(es, index, field_name, field_value):

    :param field_value: The field value of interest
    :return: The results of the query
    """"""
    body = {
        ""query"": {
            ""match"": {
                field_name: field_value
            }
        },
        ""_source"":"

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_most_popular_RL(index):
    """"""
    This function returns the most popular RL for people in a given index.

    Parameters
    ----------
    index : str
        The Elasticsearch index to search over.

    Returns
    -------
    dict
        A dictionary containing the most common RL for people in the index.
    """"""
    # TODO: Write your code here
    body = {
        ""size"":0,
        ""aggs"":{
            ""group_by_rl"":{
                ""terms"":{
                    ""field"":""ALLERGIES.raw""
                }
            }
        }
    }
    res = es.search(index=index,body=body)
    return res['aggregations']['group_by_rl'][""buckets""]

if __name__ == ""__main__"":
    print(""Most Common RL for People:"")
    print(json.dumps(get_most_popular_"
11442,"""""""
import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_most_popular_ra(index):
    """"""
    This function returns the most popular ra in a given index of clinical notes.

    Parameters
    ----------
    index : str
        The index to search over.

    Returns
    -------
    dict
        A dictionary containing the most popular ra and their counts.

    """"""
    body = {
        ""size"":0,
        ""_source"":[""RA""],
        ""aggs"":{
            ""ra"":{""terms"":{""field"":""RA"",""size"":10}}
        }
    }
    res = es.search(index=index,body=body)
    return res['aggregations']['ra'][""buckets""]

if __name__ == ""__main__"":
    print(json.dumps(get_most_popular_ra(""clinical-notes""),indent=4))"

12281,"### Generate the SQL query to extract the data from the CDR.
SELECT DISTINCT vaers_id FROM `vaers-data-2013`.vaers_vax_update WHERE vax_name = 'HEP B (RECOMBIVAX HB)' ORDER BY COUNT(DISTINCT vaers_id) DESC LIMIT 5;

### Execute the SQL query in BigQuery and save it as a table named ""hep_b"".
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `project-id.dataset_id.hep_b` AS SELECT * FROM `project-id.dataset_id.cdr_table` WHERE vaers_id IN (SELECT DISTINCT vaers_id FROM `project-id.dataset_id.cdr_table` WHERE vax_name = 'HEP B (RECOMBIVAX HB)');
